SELECT [t].[CreatedAt], [t].[ModifiedAt], [t].[Id], [t].[Name], [t].[Visible]
FROM (
    SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[CreatedAt], [a].[ModifiedAt], [a].[Name], [a].[Visible]
    FROM [ACTIVIDADES] AS [a]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
